Constraint:** The `sprintcart-pro-domain` module must NOT depend on any adapter or framework-specific code.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Ports (Interfaces) Definition\n\nFollowing the established pattern in the codebase (see `PaymentGatewayPort`, `ErpSystemPort`, `ManageCatalogUseCase`), we define both **outbound ports** and **inbound ports (use cases)**.\n\n### 2.1 Outbound Port: `WmsPort` (Driven Port)\n\n**Location:** `sprintcart-pro-domain/src/main/java/com/sprintcart/domain/ports/out/wms/WmsPort.java`\n\nThis port abstracts all outbound communication with the WMS. The domain layer calls this interface; the adapter implements it.\n\n```java\npackage com.sprintcart.domain.ports.out.wms;\n\nimport java.time.Duration;\nimport java.time.Instant;\nimport java.util.List;\nimport java.util.Objects;\nimport java.util.UUID;\nimport java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture;\n\n/**\n * Outbound port that abstracts all interactions with an external Warehouse Management System (WMS).\n * <p>\n * Implementations reside in the infrastructure/adapter layer and handle protocol-specific\n * details (REST, webhooks, message queues). The domain layer depends solely on this interface,\n * ensuring complete decoupling from any particular WMS vendor or transport mechanism.\n *\n * <h3>Resilience</h3>\n * All operations return {@link CompletableFuture}s for non-blocking execution. Implementations\n * are expected to apply timeouts, retries, and circuit breaker patterns. Failures must be\n * propagated as {@link WmsIntegrationException}s.\n */\npublic interface WmsPort {\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * Fulfillment Operations (Outbound to WMS)\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    /**\n     * Submits a fulfillment request to the WMS for processing.\n     * <p>\n     * This is typically called after an order is paid and ready for shipment.\n     * The WMS will allocate inventory, generate picking lists, and coordinate\n     * the physical fulfillment process.\n     *\n     * @param request Contains order details, shipping address, and line items.\n     * @return Future containing the WMS acknowledgment with external reference.\n     * @throws WmsIntegrationException if communication fails or WMS rejects the request.\n     */\n    CompletableFuture<FulfillmentAcknowledgment> submitFulfillmentRequest(FulfillmentRequest request)\n            throws WmsIntegrationException;\n\n    /**\n     * Queries the current fulfillment status from the WMS.\n     *\n     * @param orderId SprintCart order identifier.\n     * @return Future containing current status or empty if not found in WMS.\n     */\n    CompletableFuture<FulfillmentStatusResponse> getFulfillmentStatus(UUID orderId)\n            throws WmsIntegrationException;\n\n    /**\n     * Cancels an in-progress fulfillment request.\n     *\n     * @param orderId SprintCart order identifier.\n     * @param reason Cancellation reason for audit trail.\n     * @return Future indicating success or failure.\n     */\n    CompletableFuture<Boolean> cancelFulfillment(UUID orderId, String reason)\n            throws WmsIntegrationException;\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * Health & Diagnostics\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    /**\n     * Performs a lightweight health check against the WMS endpoint.\n     */\n    WmsHealth healthCheck();\n\n    /**\n     * Returns WMS integration metadata for observability dashboards.\n     */\n    WmsMetadata metadata();\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * Value Objects & Records\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    /**\n     * Request to initiate fulfillment for an order.\n     */\n    record FulfillmentRequest(\n            UUID orderId,\n            UUID customerId,\n            String correlationId,\n            ShippingDetails shippingDetails,\n            List<FulfillmentLineItem> lineItems,\n            FulfillmentPriority priority,\n            Instant requestedAt\n    ) {\n        public FulfillmentRequest {\n            Objects.requireNonNull(orderId, \"orderId must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(customerId, \"customerId must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(shippingDetails, \"shippingDetails must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(lineItems, \"lineItems must not be null\");\n            if (lineItems.isEmpty()) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"lineItems must not be empty\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Individual line item within a fulfillment request.\n     */\n    record FulfillmentLineItem(\n            UUID productId,\n            String sku,\n            String productName,\n            int quantity,\n            String specialInstructions\n    ) {\n        public FulfillmentLineItem {\n            Objects.requireNonNull(productId, \"productId must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(sku, \"sku must not be null\");\n            if (quantity <= 0) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"quantity must be positive\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Shipping destination details.\n     */\n    record ShippingDetails(\n            String recipientName,\n            String addressLine1,\n            String addressLine2,\n            String city,\n            String state,\n            String postalCode,\n            String country,\n            String phoneNumber,\n            String shippingMethod\n    ) {}\n\n    /**\n     * Priority level for fulfillment processing.\n     */\n    enum FulfillmentPriority {\n        STANDARD,\n        EXPRESS,\n        SAME_DAY,\n        PRIORITY\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Acknowledgment returned by WMS after accepting a fulfillment request.\n     */\n    record FulfillmentAcknowledgment(\n            String wmsReferenceId,\n            UUID orderId,\n            FulfillmentStatus status,\n            Instant acceptedAt,\n            Instant estimatedShipDate\n    ) {}\n\n    /**\n     * Current fulfillment status from WMS.\n     */\n    record FulfillmentStatusResponse(\n            UUID orderId,\n            String wmsReferenceId,\n            FulfillmentStatus status,\n            String trackingNumber,\n            String carrier,\n            Instant lastUpdated,\n            List<FulfillmentEvent> events\n    ) {}\n\n    /**\n     * Individual fulfillment milestone event.\n     */\n    record FulfillmentEvent(\n            FulfillmentStatus status,\n            String description,\n            Instant occurredAt\n    ) {}\n\n    /**\n     * Possible fulfillment states.\n     */\n    enum FulfillmentStatus {\n        RECEIVED,\n        PROCESSING,\n        PICKING,\n        PACKING,\n        SHIPPED,\n        DELIVERED,\n        CANCELED,\n        ON_HOLD,\n        FAILED\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * WMS health check result.\n     */\n    record WmsHealth(\n            HealthState state,\n            String description,\n            Duration responseTime,\n            Instant checkedAt\n    ) {\n        public enum HealthState { OK, DEGRADED, DOWN }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * WMS integration metadata.\n     */\n    record WmsMetadata(\n            String vendor,\n            String apiVersion,\n            String endpointUrl\n    ) {}\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * Exception\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    /**\n     * Exception for WMS integration failures.\n     */\n    class WmsIntegrationException extends RuntimeException {\n        private final ErrorCategory category;\n\n        public WmsIntegrationException(String message, ErrorCategory category) {\n            super(message);\n            this.category = category;\n        }\n\n        public WmsIntegrationException(String message, Throwable cause, ErrorCategory category) {\n            super(message, cause);\n            this.category = category;\n        }\n\n        public ErrorCategory category() {\n            return category;\n        }\n\n        public enum ErrorCategory {\n            NETWORK,\n            AUTHENTICATION,\n            VALIDATION,\n            RATE_LIMIT,\n            WMS_REJECTION,\n            TIMEOUT,\n            OTHER\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 2.2 Inbound Port: `UpdateStockUseCase` (Driving Port)\n\n**Location:** `sprintcart-pro-domain/src/main/java/com/sprintcart/domain/ports/in/inventory/UpdateStockUseCase.java`\n\nThis is a **Use Case** port (inbound/driving) that defines the contract for updating stock levels. The application service implements this interface; the WMS adapter's controller calls it.\n\n```java\npackage com.sprintcart.domain.ports.in.inventory;\n\nimport java.time.Instant;\nimport java.util.List;\nimport java.util.Objects;\nimport java.util.UUID;\n\n/**\n * Inbound port (Use Case) for handling stock level updates from external systems.\n * <p>\n * This interface is technology-agnostic and must be implemented by an application\n * service. External adapters (REST controllers, message consumers) invoke this\n * port to update inventory levels in the domain.\n *\n * <p><strong>Idempotency:</strong> Implementations must support idempotent operations\n * using the provided {@code correlationId} to prevent duplicate processing.\n */\npublic interface UpdateStockUseCase {\n\n    /**\n     * Processes a batch of stock updates from an external source (e.g., WMS).\n     *\n     * @param command Contains stock adjustments and metadata.\n     * @return Result indicating success/failure for each SKU.\n     * @throws InvalidStockUpdateException if validation fails.\n     */\n    StockUpdateResult updateStock(UpdateStockCommand command)\n            throws InvalidStockUpdateException;\n\n    /**\n     * Processes a single SKU stock update.\n     *\n     * @param command Single SKU update details.\n     * @return Result for the single update.\n     */\n    SingleSkuUpdateResult updateSingleSku(SingleSkuUpdateCommand command)\n            throws InvalidStockUpdateException;\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * Command Objects\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    /**\n     * Command for batch stock updates.\n     */\n    record UpdateStockCommand(\n            String correlationId,\n            String sourceSystem,\n            Instant receivedAt,\n            List<StockAdjustment> adjustments\n    ) {\n        public UpdateStockCommand {\n            Objects.requireNonNull(correlationId, \"correlationId must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(sourceSystem, \"sourceSystem must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(adjustments, \"adjustments must not be null\");\n            if (adjustments.isEmpty()) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"adjustments must not be empty\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Command for single SKU update.\n     */\n    record SingleSkuUpdateCommand(\n            String correlationId,\n            String sourceSystem,\n            String sku,\n            int newQuantity,\n            String warehouseLocation,\n            StockUpdateReason reason,\n            Instant effectiveAt\n    ) {\n        public SingleSkuUpdateCommand {\n            Objects.requireNonNull(correlationId, \"correlationId must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(sku, \"sku must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(reason, \"reason must not be null\");\n            if (newQuantity < 0) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"newQuantity cannot be negative\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Individual stock adjustment within a batch.\n     */\n    record StockAdjustment(\n            String sku,\n            int previousQuantity,\n            int newQuantity,\n            String warehouseLocation,\n            StockUpdateReason reason\n    ) {\n        public StockAdjustment {\n            Objects.requireNonNull(sku, \"sku must not be null\");\n            Objects.requireNonNull(reason, \"reason must not be null\");\n            if (newQuantity < 0) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"newQuantity cannot be negative\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Reason for stock adjustment.\n     */\n    enum StockUpdateReason {\n        WMS_SYNC,\n        GOODS_RECEIVED,\n        RETURN_PROCESSED,\n        DAMAGED,\n        CYCLE_COUNT,\n        SHRINKAGE,\n        MANUAL_ADJUSTMENT,\n        TRANSFER\n    }\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * Result Objects\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    /**\n     * Result of batch stock update.\n     */\n    record StockUpdateResult(\n            String correlationId,\n            int totalProcessed,\n            int successCount,\n            int failureCount,\n            List<SkuUpdateStatus> details,\n            Instant processedAt\n    ) {}\n\n    /**\n     * Result for single SKU update.\n     */\n    record SingleSkuUpdateResult(\n            String correlationId,\n            String sku,\n            boolean success,\n            String message,\n            int finalQuantity,\n            Instant processedAt\n    ) {}\n\n    /**\n     * Status for individual SKU within batch.\n     */\n    record SkuUpdateStatus(\n            String sku,\n            boolean success,\n            String errorMessage,\n            int finalQuantity\n    ) {}\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * Exceptions\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    /**\n     * Thrown when stock update validation fails.\n     */\n    class InvalidStockUpdateException extends Exception {\n        public InvalidStockUpdateException(String message) {\n            super(message);\n        }\n\n        public InvalidStockUpdateException(String message, Throwable cause) {\n            super(message, cause);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Adapter Implementation Plan\n\n### 3.1 Package Structure for `wms-adapter`\n\n```\nwms-adapter/\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 src/main/java/com/sprintcart/adapters/wms/\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 config/\n    \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 WmsAdapterConfiguration.java    // Spring configuration\n    \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 WmsSecurityConfiguration.java   // Webhook auth config\n    \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 WmsClientProperties.java        // @ConfigurationProperties\n    \u2502\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 inbound/                            // Driving adapters (WMS -> SprintCart)\n    \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 WmsWebhookController.java       // REST endpoint for WMS callbacks\n    \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 dto/\n    \u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 StockUpdateWebhookDto.java\n    \u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 FulfillmentStatusWebhookDto.java\n    \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 mapper/\n    \u2502       \u2514\u2500\u2500 WmsInboundMapper.java\n    \u2502\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 outbound/                           // Driven adapters (SprintCart -> WMS)\n    \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 WmsRestClient.java              // Implements WmsPort\n    \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 dto/\n    \u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 WmsFulfillmentRequestDto.java\n    \u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 WmsFulfillmentResponseDto.java\n    \u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 WmsStatusResponseDto.java\n    \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 mapper/\n    \u2502       \u2514\u2500\u2500 WmsOutboundMapper.java\n    \u2502\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 event/\n        \u2514\u2500\u2500 OrderPlacedEventListener.java   // Subscribes to OrderPlacedEvent\n```\n\n### 3.2 Outbound Adapter: `WmsRestClient`\n\n**Location:** `wms-adapter/src/main/java/com/sprintcart/adapters/wms/outbound/WmsRestClient.java`\n\n**Key Responsibilities:**\n- Implements `WmsPort` interface from domain\n- Uses `WebClient` for non-blocking HTTP calls\n- Applies resilience patterns (circuit breaker, retry, timeout)\n- Handles authentication (API key, OAuth2, etc.)\n- Maps domain objects to/from WMS API DTOs\n\n```java\npackage com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.outbound;\n\nimport com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.config.WmsClientProperties;\nimport com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.outbound.dto.*;\nimport com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.outbound.mapper.WmsOutboundMapper;\nimport com.sprintcart.domain.ports.out.wms.WmsPort;\nimport io.github.resilience4j.circuitbreaker.annotation.CircuitBreaker;\nimport io.github.resilience4j.retry.annotation.Retry;\nimport io.github.resilience4j.timelimiter.annotation.TimeLimiter;\nimport lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;\nimport lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;\nimport org.springframework.stereotype.Component;\nimport org.springframework.web.reactive.function.client.WebClient;\n\nimport java.time.Clock;\nimport java.time.Duration;\nimport java.time.Instant;\nimport java.util.UUID;\nimport java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture;\n\n/**\n * Outbound adapter implementing {@link WmsPort} for WMS API communication.\n * <p>\n * This adapter is responsible for:\n * <ul>\n *     <li>Translating domain objects to WMS API DTOs</li>\n *     <li>Making HTTP calls to the WMS REST API</li>\n *     <li>Handling errors and applying resilience patterns</li>\n *     <li>Translating WMS responses back to domain objects</li>\n * </ul>\n */\n@Slf4j\n@Component\n@RequiredArgsConstructor\npublic class WmsRestClient implements WmsPort {\n\n    private final WebClient wmsWebClient;\n    private final WmsClientProperties properties;\n    private final WmsOutboundMapper mapper;\n    private final Clock clock;\n\n    @Override\n    @CircuitBreaker(name = \"wms\", fallbackMethod = \"submitFulfillmentFallback\")\n    @Retry(name = \"wms\")\n    @TimeLimiter(name = \"wms\")\n    public CompletableFuture<FulfillmentAcknowledgment> submitFulfillmentRequest(\n            FulfillmentRequest request) {\n\n        log.info(\"Submitting fulfillment request to WMS for order {}\", request.orderId());\n\n        WmsFulfillmentRequestDto dto = mapper.toWmsRequest(request);\n\n        return wmsWebClient.post()\n                .uri(\"/v1/fulfillment/orders\")\n                .header(\"X-Idempotency-Key\", request.correlationId())\n                .header(\"X-API-Key\", properties.getApiKey())\n                .bodyValue(dto)\n                .retrieve()\n                .bodyToMono(WmsFulfillmentResponseDto.class)\n                .map(mapper::toAcknowledgment)\n                .doOnSuccess(ack -> log.info(\"WMS accepted fulfillment for order {}, WMS ref: {}\",\n                        request.orderId(), ack.wmsReferenceId()))\n                .doOnError(ex -> log.error(\"WMS fulfillment submission failed for order {}\",\n                        request.orderId(), ex))\n                .toFuture();\n    }\n\n    // Fallback method for circuit breaker\n    private CompletableFuture<FulfillmentAcknowledgment> submitFulfillmentFallback(\n            FulfillmentRequest request, Throwable throwable) {\n\n        log.warn(\"WMS circuit breaker open, returning degraded response for order {}\",\n                request.orderId());\n        throw new WmsIntegrationException(\n                \"WMS service unavailable\",\n                throwable,\n                WmsIntegrationException.ErrorCategory.NETWORK);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    @CircuitBreaker(name = \"wms\")\n    public CompletableFuture<FulfillmentStatusResponse> getFulfillmentStatus(UUID orderId) {\n        return wmsWebClient.get()\n                .uri(\"/v1/fulfillment/orders/{orderId}/status\", orderId)\n                .header(\"X-API-Key\", properties.getApiKey())\n                .retrieve()\n                .bodyToMono(WmsStatusResponseDto.class)\n                .map(mapper::toStatusResponse)\n                .toFuture();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    @CircuitBreaker(name = \"wms\")\n    public CompletableFuture<Boolean> cancelFulfillment(UUID orderId, String reason) {\n        return wmsWebClient.post()\n                .uri(\"/v1/fulfillment/orders/{orderId}/cancel\", orderId)\n                .header(\"X-API-Key\", properties.getApiKey())\n                .bodyValue(new CancelRequestDto(reason))\n                .retrieve()\n                .toBodilessEntity()\n                .map(response -> response.getStatusCode().is2xxSuccessful())\n                .toFuture();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public WmsHealth healthCheck() {\n        Instant start = clock.instant();\n        try {\n            Boolean healthy = wmsWebClient.get()\n                    .uri(\"/health\")\n                    .retrieve()\n                    .toBodilessEntity()\n                    .map(r -> r.getStatusCode().is2xxSuccessful())\n                    .block(Duration.ofSeconds(5));\n\n            return new WmsHealth(\n                    Boolean.TRUE.equals(healthy) ? WmsHealth.HealthState.OK : WmsHealth.HealthState.DEGRADED,\n                    \"WMS API responded\",\n                    Duration.between(start, clock.instant()),\n                    clock.instant()\n            );\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            return new WmsHealth(\n                    WmsHealth.HealthState.DOWN,\n                    \"WMS API unreachable: \" + e.getMessage(),\n                    Duration.between(start, clock.instant()),\n                    clock.instant()\n            );\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public WmsMetadata metadata() {\n        return new WmsMetadata(\n                properties.getVendor(),\n                properties.getApiVersion(),\n                properties.getBaseUrl()\n        );\n    }\n\n    // Internal DTO for cancel request\n    private record CancelRequestDto(String reason) {}\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3 Inbound Adapter: `WmsWebhookController`\n\n**Location:** `wms-adapter/src/main/java/com/sprintcart/adapters/wms/inbound/WmsWebhookController.java`\n\n**Key Responsibilities:**\n- Exposes REST endpoint(s) for WMS webhook callbacks\n- Validates webhook signatures for security\n- Maps incoming DTOs to use case commands\n- Delegates to application layer (not domain directly)\n- Returns appropriate HTTP responses\n\n```java\npackage com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.inbound;\n\nimport com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.inbound.dto.StockUpdateWebhookDto;\nimport com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.inbound.mapper.WmsInboundMapper;\nimport com.sprintcart.domain.ports.in.inventory.UpdateStockUseCase;\nimport com.sprintcart.domain.ports.in.inventory.UpdateStockUseCase.*;\nimport jakarta.validation.Valid;\nimport lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;\nimport lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;\nimport org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;\nimport org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;\nimport org.springframework.validation.annotation.Validated;\nimport org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;\n\nimport java.time.Instant;\n\n/**\n * Inbound adapter (REST controller) that handles WMS webhook callbacks.\n * <p>\n * This controller is deliberately thin - it validates requests, maps DTOs to\n * domain commands, and delegates all business logic to the application layer\n * via the {@link UpdateStockUseCase} port.\n *\n * <h3>Security</h3>\n * Endpoints are secured via HMAC signature validation configured in\n * {@code WmsSecurityConfiguration}. The WMS must sign requests with a\n * shared secret.\n */\n@Slf4j\n@RestController\n@RequestMapping(\"/api/v1/wms/webhooks\")\n@RequiredArgsConstructor\n@Validated\npublic class WmsWebhookController {\n\n    private final UpdateStockUseCase updateStockUseCase;\n    private final WmsInboundMapper mapper;\n\n    /**\n     * Endpoint for WMS to push stock level updates.\n     * <p>\n     * The WMS calls this endpoint whenever inventory levels change\n     * (goods received, shipments, cycle counts, etc.).\n     *\n     * @param signature    HMAC signature from X-WMS-Signature header\n     * @param webhookId    Unique webhook event ID for idempotency\n     * @param payload      Stock update payload from WMS\n     * @return Acknowledgment with processing results\n     */\n    @PostMapping(\"/stock-updates\")\n    public ResponseEntity<StockUpdateResponseDto> handleStockUpdate(\n            @RequestHeader(value = \"X-WMS-Signature\", required = true) String signature,\n            @RequestHeader(value = \"X-WMS-Webhook-Id\", required = true) String webhookId,\n            @Valid @RequestBody StockUpdateWebhookDto payload) {\n\n        log.info(\"Received stock update webhook from WMS. Webhook ID: {}, SKU count: {}\",\n                webhookId, payload.getAdjustments().size());\n\n        try {\n            // Map DTO to domain command\n            UpdateStockCommand command = mapper.toCommand(payload, webhookId);\n\n            // Delegate to application layer use case\n            StockUpdateResult result = updateStockUseCase.updateStock(command);\n\n            log.info(\"Stock update processed. Webhook ID: {}, Success: {}/{}, Failures: {}\",\n                    webhookId, result.successCount(), result.totalProcessed(), result.failureCount());\n\n            return ResponseEntity.ok(new StockUpdateResponseDto(\n                    webhookId,\n                    result.successCount(),\n                    result.failureCount(),\n                    result.processedAt()\n            ));\n\n        } catch (InvalidStockUpdateException e) {\n            log.warn(\"Invalid stock update from WMS. Webhook ID: {}, Error: {}\",\n                    webhookId, e.getMessage());\n            return ResponseEntity.badRequest()\n                    .body(new StockUpdateResponseDto(webhookId, 0, payload.getAdjustments().size(),\n                            Instant.now(), e.getMessage()));\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Endpoint for WMS to push fulfillment status updates.\n     * <p>\n     * Called when fulfillment status changes (picked, packed, shipped, etc.).\n     */\n    @PostMapping(\"/fulfillment-status\")\n    public ResponseEntity<Void> handleFulfillmentStatus(\n            @RequestHeader(value = \"X-WMS-Signature\", required = true) String signature,\n            @RequestHeader(value = \"X-WMS-Webhook-Id\", required = true) String webhookId,\n            @Valid @RequestBody FulfillmentStatusWebhookDto payload) {\n\n        log.info(\"Received fulfillment status update from WMS. Order: {}, Status: {}\",\n                payload.getOrderId(), payload.getStatus());\n\n        // Delegate to appropriate use case for status update handling\n        // This would update order status and emit domain events\n\n        return ResponseEntity.accepted().build();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Health check endpoint for WMS to verify connectivity.\n     */\n    @GetMapping(\"/health\")\n    public ResponseEntity<String> healthCheck() {\n        return ResponseEntity.ok(\"OK\");\n    }\n\n    // Response DTOs\n\n    public record StockUpdateResponseDto(\n            String webhookId,\n            int successCount,\n            int failureCount,\n            Instant processedAt,\n            String errorMessage\n    ) {\n        public StockUpdateResponseDto(String webhookId, int successCount, int failureCount, Instant processedAt) {\n            this(webhookId, successCount, failureCount, processedAt, null);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.4 Event Listener: `OrderPlacedEventListener`\n\n**Location:** `wms-adapter/src/main/java/com/sprintcart/adapters/wms/event/OrderPlacedEventListener.java`\n\nThis component subscribes to `OrderPlacedEvent` domain events and triggers WMS fulfillment requests.\n\n```java\npackage com.sprintcart.adapters.wms.event;\n\nimport com.sprintcart.application.service.DomainEventProcessor.DomainEvent;\nimport com.sprintcart.application.service.DomainEventProcessor.DomainEventSubscriber;\nimport com.sprintcart.domain.events.OrderPlacedEvent;\nimport com.sprintcart.domain.ports.out.wms.WmsPort;\nimport com.sprintcart.domain.ports.out.wms.WmsPort.*;\nimport lombok.NonNull;\nimport lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;\nimport lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;\nimport org.springframework.stereotype.Component;\n\nimport java.time.Instant;\nimport java.util.stream.Collectors;\n\n/**\n * Domain event subscriber that listens for {@link OrderPlacedEvent}s and\n * triggers fulfillment requests to the WMS.\n * <p>\n * This follows the event-driven pattern established by the existing\n * {@link com.sprintcart.application.service.DomainEventProcessor}.\n */\n@Slf4j\n@Component\n@RequiredArgsConstructor\npublic class OrderPlacedEventListener implements DomainEventSubscriber<OrderPlacedEvent> {\n\n    private final WmsPort wmsPort;\n\n    @Override\n    public void handle(@NonNull OrderPlacedEvent event) {\n        log.info(\"Processing OrderPlacedEvent for order {}\", event.getOrderId());\n\n        FulfillmentRequest request = mapToFulfillmentRequest(event);\n\n        wmsPort.submitFulfillmentRequest(request)\n                .thenAccept(ack -> log.info(\"WMS acknowledged fulfillment for order {}. WMS Ref: {}\",\n                        event.getOrderId(), ack.wmsReferenceId()))\n                .exceptionally(ex -> {\n                    log.error(\"Failed to submit fulfillment to WMS for order {}\",\n                            event.getOrderId(), ex);\n                    // In production: publish to DLQ or retry queue\n                    return null;\n                });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean supports(@NonNull Class<? extends DomainEvent> eventType) {\n        return OrderPlacedEvent.class.equals(eventType);\n    }\n\n    private FulfillmentRequest mapToFulfillmentRequest(OrderPlacedEvent event) {\n        var lineItems = event.getOrderLines().stream()\n                .map(line -> new FulfillmentLineItem(\n                        line.getProductId(),\n                        line.getSku(),\n                        line.getSku(), // Product name would come from enrichment\n                        line.getQuantity(),\n                        null\n                ))\n                .collect(Collectors.toList());\n\n        // ShippingDetails would be fetched from Order aggregate or enriched\n        ShippingDetails shippingDetails = new ShippingDetails(\n                \"Customer Name\", // Would come from order/customer service\n                \"Address Line 1\",\n                null,\n                \"City\",\n                \"State\",\n                \"12345\",\n                \"US\",\n                null,\n                \"STANDARD\"\n        );\n\n        return new FulfillmentRequest(\n                event.getOrderId(),\n                event.getCustomerId(),\n                event.getCorrelationId() != null ? event.getCorrelationId() : event.eventId().toString(),\n                shippingDetails,\n                lineItems,\n                FulfillmentPriority.STANDARD,\n                Instant.now()\n        );\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Application Layer Orchestration\n\n### 4.1 Modifications to `CatalogService`\n\nThe `CatalogService` in `sprintcart-pro-application` should implement the `UpdateStockUseCase` interface to handle inbound stock updates from the WMS.\n\n**Location:** `sprintcart-pro-application/src/main/java/com/sprintcart/application/service/CatalogService.java`\n\n**Required Changes:**\n\n```java\npackage com.sprintcart.application.service;\n\n// ... existing imports ...\nimport com.sprintcart.domain.ports.in.inventory.UpdateStockUseCase;\n\n/**\n * Application service that orchestrates catalog-related use-cases.\n * Now also implements UpdateStockUseCase for WMS stock updates.\n */\n@Slf4j\n@Service\n@RequiredArgsConstructor\npublic class CatalogService implements UpdateStockUseCase {\n\n    private final CatalogPort catalogPort;\n    private final AdvertisementPort advertisementPort;\n    private final EventPublisher eventPublisher;\n    private final Validator validator;\n    private final Clock clock;\n\n    // ... existing methods ...\n\n    /* ========================================================================\n     * UpdateStockUseCase Implementation (for WMS integration)\n     * ======================================================================== */\n\n    @Override\n    @Transactional\n    public StockUpdateResult updateStock(UpdateStockCommand command) throws InvalidStockUpdateException {\n        log.info(\"Processing batch stock update. Correlation: {}, Adjustments: {}\",\n                command.correlationId(), command.adjustments().size());\n\n        // Check for duplicate processing (idempotency)\n        if (isAlreadyProcessed(command.correlationId())) {\n            log.info(\"Duplicate stock update ignored. Correlation: {}\", command.correlationId());\n            return getPreviousResult(command.correlationId());\n        }\n\n        List<SkuUpdateStatus> results = new ArrayList<>();\n        int successCount = 0;\n\n        for (StockAdjustment adjustment : command.adjustments()) {\n            try {\n                updateProductStock(adjustment);\n                results.add(new SkuUpdateStatus(adjustment.sku(), true, null, adjustment.newQuantity()));\n                successCount++;\n\n                // Check for low stock and trigger automations\n                checkLowStockThreshold(adjustment.sku(), adjustment.newQuantity());\n\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                log.warn(\"Failed to update stock for SKU {}. Error: {}\", adjustment.sku(), e.getMessage());\n                results.add(new SkuUpdateStatus(adjustment.sku(), false, e.getMessage(), -1));\n            }\n        }\n\n        StockUpdateResult result = new StockUpdateResult(\n                command.correlationId(),\n                command.adjustments().size(),\n                successCount,\n                command.adjustments().size() - successCount,\n                results,\n                Instant.now(clock)\n        );\n\n        // Store result for idempotency checks\n        storeProcessedResult(command.correlationId(), result);\n\n        log.info(\"Batch stock update completed. Success: {}, Failures: {}\",\n                result.successCount(), result.failureCount());\n\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    @Transactional\n    public SingleSkuUpdateResult updateSingleSku(SingleSkuUpdateCommand command)\n            throws InvalidStockUpdateException {\n        log.info(\"Processing single SKU stock update. SKU: {}, New Qty: {}\",\n                command.sku(), command.newQuantity());\n\n        try {\n            StockAdjustment adjustment = new StockAdjustment(\n                    command.sku(),\n                    -1, // Previous quantity unknown for single update\n                    command.newQuantity(),\n                    command.warehouseLocation(),\n                    command.reason()\n            );\n\n            updateProductStock(adjustment);\n            checkLowStockThreshold(command.sku(), command.newQuantity());\n\n            return new SingleSkuUpdateResult(\n                    command.correlationId(),\n                    command.sku(),\n                    true,\n                    \"Stock updated successfully\",\n                    command.newQuantity(),\n                    Instant.now(clock)\n            );\n\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            throw new InvalidStockUpdateException(\"Failed to update SKU \" + command.sku() + \": \" + e.getMessage(), e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void updateProductStock(StockAdjustment adjustment) {\n        // Use existing CatalogPort to update product inventory\n        catalogPort.updateStockBySku(adjustment.sku(), adjustment.newQuantity(), adjustment.warehouseLocation());\n    }\n\n    private void checkLowStockThreshold(String sku, int newQuantity) {\n        // Emit LowStockEvent if below threshold (existing logic)\n        catalogPort.findBySku(sku).ifPresent(product -> {\n            product.getInventory().ifPresent(inventory -> {\n                if (newQuantity < inventory.reorderThreshold()) {\n                    log.info(\"Low stock detected for SKU {}. Qty: {}, Threshold: {}\",\n                            sku, newQuantity, inventory.reorderThreshold());\n                    advertisementPort.pauseCampaignsForProduct(product.getId());\n                    eventPublisher.publishAsync(new LowStockEvent(\n                            product.getId(), newQuantity, inventory.reorderThreshold(), Instant.now(clock)));\n                }\n            });\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Idempotency helpers (would use Redis/database in production)\n    private boolean isAlreadyProcessed(String correlationId) {\n        // Implementation would check persistent store\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    private StockUpdateResult getPreviousResult(String correlationId) {\n        // Implementation would retrieve from persistent store\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    private void storeProcessedResult(String correlationId, StockUpdateResult result) {\n        // Implementation would persist for idempotency\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 4.2 Sequence of Calls\n\n#### Outbound Flow: Order Placed -> WMS Fulfillment\n\n```\n1. Customer completes checkout\n2. OrderController.createOrder() is called\n3. OrderService.placeOrder() persists order and publishes OrderPlacedEvent\n4. DomainEventProcessor.process() receives the event\n5. OrderPlacedEventListener.handle() is invoked\n6. OrderPlacedEventListener maps event to FulfillmentRequest\n7. WmsPort.submitFulfillmentRequest() is called\n8. WmsRestClient (adapter) makes HTTP POST to WMS API\n9. WMS responds with FulfillmentAcknowledgment\n10. Listener logs success (or handles failure)\n```\n\n#### Inbound Flow: WMS Stock Update -> SprintCart\n\n```\n1. WMS detects inventory change (goods received, shipment, etc.)\n2. WMS calls POST /api/v1/wms/webhooks/stock-updates\n3. WmsWebhookController validates signature and parses request\n4. Controller maps DTO to UpdateStockCommand\n5. Controller calls UpdateStockUseCase.updateStock()\n6. CatalogService (implementing use case) processes each adjustment\n7. CatalogPort.updateStockBySku() updates database\n8. Low stock check triggers LowStockEvent if needed\n9. Controller returns StockUpdateResponseDto to WMS\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. 5.2 Primary Components Summary\n\n| Step | Component | Module | Responsibility |\n|------|-----------|--------|----------------|\n| 1 | `WmsSecurityFilter` | wms-adapter | HMAC signature validation |\n| 2 | `WmsWebhookController` | wms-adapter | HTTP request handling, validation |\n| 3 | `WmsInboundMapper` | wms-adapter | DTO to command mapping |\n| 4 | `CatalogService` | application | Business orchestration, transactions |\n| 5 | `ProductRepositoryAdapter` | persistence-adapter | Database operations |\n| 6 | `EventPublisher` | application | Domain event emission |\n| 7 | `ElasticsearchAdapter` | search-adapter | Search index update |\n| 8 | PostgreSQL | infrastructure | Data persistence |\n\n---\n\n## 6. Architectural Justification\n\n### 6.1 Reference: ADR-001 Hexagonal Architecture\n\nFrom `docs/architecture/adr/001-hexagonal-architecture.md`:\n\n> **Decision:** We will structure SprintCart Pro following _Hexagonal Architecture_ (Ports & Adapters) as described by Alistair Cockburn:\n> - **Domain Layer (Inside)** \u2014 Aggregates, Entities, Value Objects, and Domain Services with no dependencies on frameworks.\n> - **Application Layer** \u2014 Use-cases (Service Layer) orchestrating domain objects via _inbound ports_ (commands/queries).\n> - **Inbound Adapters** \u2014 REST/GraphQL controllers, WebSocket handlers, scheduled jobs.\n> - **Outbound Adapters** \u2014 Payment gateways, messaging, notification services, external ERPs.\n> - **Ports** \u2014 Java interfaces owned by the core that define required/expected behavior, enabling adapters to plug in without touching the domain.\n\n**How This Plan Aligns:**\n\n1. **Domain Layer Purity**: The new `WmsPort` and `UpdateStockUseCase` interfaces are defined in `sprintcart-pro-domain` with zero framework dependencies. They use pure Java records and standard library types only.\n\n2. **Port Ownership**: Both ports are \"owned by the core\" (domain module). The adapter module depends on domain, not vice versa, respecting the dependency inversion principle.\n\n3. **Inbound vs Outbound Distinction**:\n   - `UpdateStockUseCase` is an **inbound port** (driving) - defines what the outside world can ask the system to do\n   - `WmsPort` is an **outbound port** (driven) - defines what the system needs from the external world\n\n4. **Adapter Isolation**: All WMS-specific code (REST client, webhooks, DTOs, security) is isolated in the new `wms-adapter` module, matching the pattern of existing adapters like `payment-adapter` and `notification-adapter`.\n\n### 6.2 Reference: C4 Component Diagram\n\nFrom `docs/architecture/c4-model/03_component_diagram.puml`:\n\n```\nComponent(erpAdapter, \"ERPAdapter\", \"REST/JSON Client\",\n          \"Syncs inventory & invoices with ERP.\", $tags = \"Outbound\")\n```\n\nThe C4 diagram shows existing outbound adapters (PaymentGatewayAdapter, ERPAdapter, EmailNotificationAdapter) as separate components that:\n- Implement domain-defined ports\n- Use technology-specific SDKs/clients\n- Are tagged as \"Outbound\" in the architectural model\n\n**How This Plan Aligns:**\n\nThe proposed `WmsRestClient` follows the exact same pattern as `ERPAdapter`:\n- Lives in an adapter module\n- Implements a domain port (`WmsPort`)\n- Uses `WebClient` for HTTP communication\n- Is tagged as \"Outbound\" in the architecture\n\nSimilarly, `WmsWebhookController` follows the pattern of `apiGateway`:\n- Lives in an adapter module\n- Is an \"Inbound\" component\n- Delegates to application services via use case ports\n- Does not contain business logic\n\n### 6.3 Dependency Rule Compliance\n\nFrom ADR-001:\n\n> The domain, application, and adapter layers compile independently, are wired by Spring Boot in the `sprintcart-boot` module, and can be sliced for serverless or on-prem deployments.\n\n**Verification of Dependency Direction:**\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502                      DEPENDENCY FLOW                        \u2502\n\u2502                                                             \u2502\n\u2502   wms-adapter \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25ba sprintcart-pro-application        \u2502\n\u2502       \u2502                           \u2502                         \u2502\n\u2502       \u2502                           \u2502                         \u2502\n\u2502       \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u25ba sprintcart-pro-domain\u2502\n\u2502                                   \u2502           \u2502             \u2502\n\u2502                                   \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518             \u2502\n\u2502                                                             \u2502\n\u2502   Dependencies ALWAYS point INWARD (toward domain)          \u2502\n\u2502   Domain has ZERO outward dependencies                      \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\nThe domain module:\n- Defines `WmsPort` interface (outbound)\n- Defines `UpdateStockUseCase` interface (inbound)\n- Has NO knowledge of REST, WebClient, Spring, or WMS API specifics\n\nThe application module:\n- Implements `UpdateStockUseCase` in `CatalogService`\n- Uses `WmsPort` via dependency injection\n- Has NO knowledge of HTTP or WMS API specifics\n\nThe adapter module:\n- Implements `WmsPort` in `WmsRestClient`\n- Calls `UpdateStockUseCase` from `WmsWebhookController`\n- Contains ALL WMS-specific and HTTP-specific code\n\nThis strict layering ensures that:\n1. Domain logic can be tested with mock ports\n2. WMS vendor can be swapped by implementing a new adapter\n3. Transport mechanisms (REST, gRPC, message queue) can change without affecting business logic\n\n---\n\n## 7. Summary\n\nThis technical plan outlines a complete, architecturally-compliant approach to integrating a third-party WMS with SprintCart Pro. Key design decisions include:\n\n| Aspect | Decision | Justification |\n|--------|----------|---------------|\n| **New Module** | `wms-adapter` under `sprintcart-pro-adapters` | Follows existing adapter module pattern |\n| **Outbound Port** | `WmsPort` in domain module | Abstracts WMS API, enables vendor swapping |\n| **Inbound Port** | `UpdateStockUseCase` in domain module | Use case pattern for stock updates |\n| **Event Integration** | `OrderPlacedEventListener` | Decoupled fulfillment trigger via domain events |\n| **Resilience** | Resilience4j circuit breaker, retry | Production-grade fault tolerance |\n| **Security** | HMAC signature validation | Webhook authentication |\n| **Idempotency** | Correlation ID tracking | Prevents duplicate processing |\n\nThe design strictly adheres to:\n- ADR-001 Hexagonal Architecture principles\n- C4 model component structure\n- Existing codebase patterns and conventions\n",

# Technical Plan: Warehouse Management System (WMS) Integration for SprintCart Pro

## Executive Summary

This document presents a detailed technical plan for integrating a third-party Warehouse Management System (WMS) into the SprintCart Pro e-commerce platform. The integration supports two critical business capabilities:

1. **Outbound Fulfillment Request**: When an order is successfully paid and confirmed, SprintCart Pro sends fulfillment details to the WMS API.
2. **Inbound Stock Update**: SprintCart Pro exposes a secure endpoint for the WMS to push real-time stock level updates.

This plan strictly adheres to the Hexagonal Architecture (Ports & Adapters) pattern established in ADR-001 and maintains consistency with existing C4 model documentation.

---

## 1. Module and Dependency Strategy

### 1.1 New Maven Module Required

A new adapter module should be created under the `sprintcart-pro-adapters` parent:

```
sprintcart-pro-adapters/
├── notification-adapter/
├── payment-adapter/
├── persistence-adapter/
├── search-adapter/
├── web-adapter/
└── wms-adapter/          <-- NEW MODULE
```

**Module Name:** `sprintcart-pro-adapters-wms`
**Artifact ID:** `wms-adapter`

### 1.2 Module Dependencies

#### New `wms-adapter` Module Dependencies

```xml
<dependencies>
    <!-- Internal Hexagonal Layers -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>com.sprintcart.pro</groupId>
        <artifactId>sprintcart-pro-domain</artifactId>
        <version>${project.version}</version>
    </dependency>
    <dependency>
        <groupId>com.sprintcart.pro</groupId>
        <artifactId>sprintcart-pro-application</artifactId>
        <version>${project.version}</version>
    </dependency>

    <!-- HTTP Client for outbound WMS calls -->
    <dependency>
        <groupId>org.springframework.boot<
... (truncated)
